       <div data-title="Match object" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="257">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="258">
         <h3 id="match-object">Match object</h3> 
         <p>A match object is a <a href="#route-object">Route object</a> with an additional confidence field.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>confidence</code>: a number between <code>0</code> (low) and <code>1</code> (high) indicating level of confidence in the returned match</li> 
         </ul> 
         <p>Refer to the <a href="#route-object">Route object</a> documentation for how the rest of a <a href="#match-object">Match object</a> is structured.</p> 
        </div>
        <div class="space-bottom4 col6 pad2 prose clip fill-light space-top5" data-reactid="259">
         <h4 id="example-match-object">Example Match object</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">{
    <span class="hljs-attr">"confidence"</span>: <span class="hljs-number">0.9548844020537051</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"distance"</span>: <span class="hljs-number">103.7</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"duration"</span>: <span class="hljs-number">16.4</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"geometry"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"gatfEfidjUi@Le@@Y?E??J?^Hf@"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"legs"</span>: []
}</pre> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Tracepoint object" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="260">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="261">
         <h3 id="tracepoint-object">Tracepoint object</h3> 
         <p>A tracepoint object is <a href="#waypoint-object">Waypoint object</a> with two additional fields:</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>matchings_index</code>: Index to the <code>match object</code> in matchings the sub-trace was matched to.</li> 
          <li><code>waypoint_index</code>: Index of the waypoint inside the matched route.</li> 
          <li><code>alternatives_count</code>: Number of probable alternative matchings for this trace point. A value of zero indicates that this point was matched unambiguously. Split the trace at these points for incremental map matching.</li> 
         </ul> 
        </div>
        <div class="space-bottom4 col6 pad2 prose clip fill-light space-top5" data-reactid="262">
         <h4 id="example-tracepoint-object">Example Tracepoint object</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">{
    <span class="hljs-attr">"waypoint_index"</span>: <span class="hljs-number">0</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"location"</span>: [<span class="hljs-number">-117.172836</span>, <span class="hljs-number">32.71204</span>],
    <span class="hljs-attr">"name"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"North Harbor Drive"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"matchings_index"</span>: <span class="hljs-number">0</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"alternatives_count"</span>: <span class="hljs-number">0</span>
}</pre> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Map Matching errors" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="263">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="264">
         <h3 id="map-matching-errors">Map Matching errors</h3> 
         <p>On error, the server responds with different HTTP status codes. For responses with HTTP status codes lower than <code>500</code>, the JSON response body includes the code property, which may be used by client programs to manage control flow. The response body may also include a message property, with a human-readable explaination of the error. If a server error occurs, the HTTP status code will be 500 or higher and the response will not include a <code>code</code> property.</p> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Code option</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>Ok</code></td> 
            <td>Normal case</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>NoMatch</code></td> 
            <td>The input did not produce any matches. <code>features</code> will be an empty array.</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>TooManyCoordinates</code></td> 
            <td>There are more than 100 points in the request.</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>InvalidInput</code></td> 
            <td><code>message</code> will hold an explanation of the invalid input.</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>ProfileNotFound</code></td> 
            <td>Needs to be a valid profile. See valid profiles <a href="#retrieve-a-match">above</a> .</td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <p>This documentation is for the <code>v5</code> API. <a href="./pages/map_matching_v4.html">See the documentation for the <code>v4</code> API</a>.</p> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Matrix" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="265">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="266">
         <h2 id="matrix">Matrix</h2> 
         <p><a id="directions-matrix"></a></p> 
         <p>The Matrix API returns travel times between many points.</p> 
         <p>For example, given 3 locations A, B, C, the Matrix API will return a matrix of all travel times in seconds between the locations:</p> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th></th> 
            <th>A</th> 
            <th>B</th> 
            <th>C</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> 
           <tr> 
            <td>A</td> 
            <td>A ? A</td> 
            <td>A ? B</td> 
            <td>A ? C</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td>B</td> 
            <td>B ? A</td> 
            <td>B ? B</td> 
            <td>B ? C</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td>C</td> 
            <td>C ? A</td> 
            <td>C ? B</td> 
            <td>C ? C</td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <p>The Matrix API will always return the duration on the fastest route. Durations between points may not be symmetric (for example A to B may have a different duration than B to A), as the routes may differ by direction due to one-way streets or turn restrictions. The Matrix API returns durations in seconds. It does not return route geometries or distances.</p> 
         <p>This API allows you to build tools that efficiently check the reachability of coordinates from each other, filter<a href="https://mapbox.com/help/define-filter/" title="A filter, also known as a predicate within iOS and macOS, gives you fine-grained control over the content of a style layer. A style layer that gets its features from a GeoJSON or vector source only includes the features that meet the filter or predicate condition that you define. See the documentation for filters and <a href=&quot;https://www.mapbox.com/ios-sdk/api/3.5.4/Classes/MGLVectorStyleLayer.html#/c:objc(cs)MGLVectorStyleLayer(py)predicate&quot;>predicates</a> for more information." class="auto-glossary-link" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank">?</a> points by travel time, or run your own algorithms for solving optimization problems.</p> 
         <p><strong>Restrictions and limits</strong></p> 
         <ul> 
          <li>Requests using <code>mapbox/driving</code>, <code>mapbox/walking</code>, and <code>mapbox/cycling</code> profiles can specify up to 25 input coordinates per request. Requests using the <code>mapbox/driving-traffic</code> profiles can specify up to 10 input coordinates per request.</li> 
          <li>Requests using <code>mapbox/driving</code>, <code>mapbox/walking</code>, and <code>mapbox/cycling</code> profiles have a maximum limit of 60 requests per minute. Requests using the <code>mapbox/driving-traffic</code> profiles have a maximum of 30 requests per minute.</li> 
         </ul> 
         <p>For example you can request a symmetric 25x25 matrix, an asymmetric 1x24 matrix with distinct coordinates or a 12x24 where sources and destinations share some coordinates.</p> 
         <p>For higher volumes, <a href="https://www.mapbox.com/contact/">contact us</a>.</p> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Retrieve a matrix" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="267">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="268">
         <h3 id="retrieve-a-matrix">Retrieve a matrix</h3> 
         <p>Returns a duration matrix showing travel times between coordinates.</p> 
         <p>The <code>{profile}</code> parameter of your request should be a Mapbox Directions routing profile<a href="https://mapbox.com/help/define-routing-profile/" title="A routing profile is a set of rules that a routing engine (like the Mapbox Directions API) uses to find the optimal route between two points. Routing profiles are generally optimized for the mode of transportation being used to get between locations." class="auto-glossary-link" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank">?</a> ID. The following IDs are supported:</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>mapbox/driving</code> for car travel times</li> 
          <li><code>mapbox/walking</code> for pedestrian and hiking travel times</li> 
          <li><code>mapbox/cycling</code> for bicycle travel times</li> 
          <li><code>mapbox/driving-traffic</code> for car travel times with traffic</li> 
         </ul> 
         <p>The <code>{coordinates}</code> parameter is a semicolon-separated list of <code>{longitude},{latitude}</code> coordinates. There must be between 2 and 25 coordinates.</p> 
         <p>In the default case, the matrix returns a symmetric matrix, using all input coordinates as sources and destinations. You may also generate an asymmetric matrix, with only some coordinates as sources or destinations:</p> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Query Parameter</th> 
            <th>Values</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>sources</code> <br> (optional)</td> 
            <td><code>{index};{index}[;{index} ...]</code> or <code>all</code> (default)</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>destinations</code> <br> (optional)</td> 
            <td><code>{index};{index}[;{index} ...]</code> or <code>all</code> (default)</td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <p>Unrecognized options in the query string result in an <code>InvalidInput</code> error.</p> 
        </div>
        <div class="space-bottom4 col6 pad2 prose clip fill-light space-top5" data-reactid="269">
         <div class="endpoint dark fill-dark round "> 
          <div class="round-left pad0y pad1x fill-lighten0 code small endpoint-method">
           GET
          </div> 
          <div class="pad0 code small endpoint-url">
           /directions-matrix/v1/
           <span class="strong">{profile}</span>/
           <span class="strong">{coordinates}</span>
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <h4 id="example-requests">Example requests</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs"><span class="hljs-comment"># request a symmetric 3x3 matrix for cars</span>
curl <span class="hljs-string">"https://api.mapbox.com/directions-matrix/v1/mapbox/driving/-122.42,37.78;-122.45,37.91;-122.48,37.73?access_token=<span class="token-widget"></span>"</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># request an asymmetric 2x3 matrix for bicycles</span>
curl <span class="hljs-string">"https://api.mapbox.com/directions-matrix/v1/mapbox/cycling/-122.42,37.78;-122.45,37.91;-122.48,37.73?sources=0;2&amp;destinations=all&amp;access_token=<span class="token-widget"></span>"</span></pre> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Matrix response format" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="270">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="271">
         <h3 id="matrix-response-format">Matrix response format</h3> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>code</code>: String indicating the state of the response. This is a separate code than the HTTP status code. On normal valid responses, the value will be <code>Ok</code>. See the errors section below for more information.</li> 
          <li><code>durations</code>: Durations as array of arrays representing the matrix in row-major order. <code>durations[i][j]</code> gives the travel time from the i-th source to the j-th destination. All values are in seconds. The duration between the same coordinate is always <code>0</code>. If a duration can not be found, the result is <code>null</code>.</li> 
          <li><code>destinations:</code>: Array of <code>waypoint</code> objects. Each waypoints is an input coordinate snapped to the road and path network. The waypoints appear in the array in the order of the input coordinates, or in the order as specified in the <code>destinations</code> query parameter.</li> 
          <li><code>sources</code>: Array of <code>waypoint</code> objects. Each waypoints is an input coordinate snapped to the road and path network. The waypoints appear in the array in the order of the input coordinates, or in the order as specified in the <code>sources</code> query parameter.</li> 
         </ul> 
        </div>
        <div class="space-bottom4 col6 pad2 prose clip fill-light space-top5" data-reactid="272">
         <h4 id="example-response-25">Example response</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">{
    <span class="hljs-attr">"code"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"Ok"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"durations"</span>: [
        [ <span class="hljs-number">0</span>,    <span class="hljs-number">77.3</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">null</span> ],
        [ <span class="hljs-number">75.7</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>,    <span class="hljs-literal">null</span> ],
        [ <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>    ]

            <span class="hljs-attr">"location"</span>: [

        },
        {

        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Matrix errors" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="273">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="274">
         <h3 id="matrix-errors">Matrix errors</h3> 
         <p>On error, the server responds with different HTTP status codes. For responses with HTTP status codes lower than <code>500</code>, the JSON response body includes the <code>code</code> property, which may be used by client programs to manage control flow. The response body may also include a <code>message</code> property, with a human-readable explanation of the error. If a server error occurs, the HTTP status code will be 500 or higher and the response will not include a <code>code</code> property.</p> 
         <p>Note that in cases where no route is found between a source<a href="https://mapbox.com/help/define-source/" title="A source supplies data to be shown on maps that use Mapbox GL. Sources are defined by the Mapbox Style Specification, and are used with style layers to visually represent the source data on to a map. Specific source types may not be supported depending on which platform you're developing on, so refer to platform-specific documentation when adding sources to your map." class="auto-glossary-link" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank">?</a> and destination, no error will be returned, but instead the respective value in the <code>durations</code> matrix will be <code>null</code>.</p> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Response body <code>code</code></th> 
            <th>HTTP status code</th> 
            <th>comment</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>Ok</code></td> 
            <td><code>200</code></td> 
            <td>Normal success case</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>ProfileNotFound</code></td> 
            <td><code>404</code></td> 
            <td>Use a valid profile as described <a href="#retrieve-a-matrix">above</a></td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>InvalidInput</code></td> 
            <td><code>422</code></td> 
            <td>The given request was not valid. The <code>message</code> key of the response will hold an explanation of the invalid input.</td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <p>The earlier Mapbox Distance API is deprecated. <a href="./pages/distances_v1.html">See the documentation</a>.</p> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Optimization" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="275">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="276">
         <h2 id="optimization">Optimization</h2> 
         <p><a id="optimized-trips"></a></p> 
         <p>The Optimization API returns a duration-optimized route between the input coordinates. This is also known as solving the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Travelling_salesman_problem">Traveling Salesperson Problem</a>. A typical use case for this API is planning the route for deliveries in a city. Route can be retrieved for car driving, bicycling and walking or hiking.</p> 
         <p><strong>Limits</strong></p> 
         <ul> 
          <li>Maximum 12 coordinates</li> 
          <li>Maximum 25 distributions per requests</li> 
          <li>Maximum 60 requests per minute</li> 
         </ul> 
         <p>For higher volumes, <a href="https://www.mapbox.com/contact/">contact us</a>.</p> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Retrieve an optimization" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="277">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="278">
         <h3 id="retrieve-an-optimization">Retrieve an optimization</h3> 
         <p>The <code>{profile}</code> parameter of your request should be a Mapbox Directions routing profile<a href="https://mapbox.com/help/define-routing-profile/" title="A routing profile is a set of rules that a routing engine (like the Mapbox Directions API) uses to find the optimal route between two points. Routing profiles are generally optimized for the mode of transportation being used to get between locations." class="auto-glossary-link" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank">?</a> ID. The following IDs are supported:</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>mapbox/driving</code> for car trips</li> 
          <li><code>mapbox/walking</code> for pedestrian and hiking trips</li> 
          <li><code>mapbox/cycling</code> for bicycle trips</li> 
         </ul> 
         <p>The <code>mapbox/driving-traffic</code> profile is not supported.</p> 
         <p>The <code>{coordinates}</code> parameter is a semicolon-separated list of <code>{longitude},{latitude}</code> coordinates. There must be between 2 and 12 coordinates. The first coordinate is the start and end point of the trip.</p> 
         <p>The response may be altered with optional query parameters:</p> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Query Parameter</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>roundtrip</code> <br> (optional)</td> 
            <td>Returned route is a roundtrip (route returns to first location). Allowed values are: <code>true</code> (default), <code>false</code> . If the roundtrip is set to <code>false</code> , then <code>source</code> and <code>destination</code> parameters are required but not all combinations are possible. See Fixing Start and End Points for additional notes.</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>source</code> <br> (optional)</td> 
            <td>Returned route starts at <code>any</code> or <code>first</code> coordinate. Allowed values are: <code>any</code> (default), <code>first</code> .</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>destination</code> <br> (optional)</td> 
            <td>Returned route ends at <code>any</code> or <code>last</code> coordinate. Allowed values are: <code>any</code> (default), <code>last</code> .</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>geometries</code> <br> (optional)</td> 
            <td>Format of the returned geometries. Allowed values are: <code>polyline</code> (default, <a href="https://developers.google.com/maps/documentation/utilities/polylinealgorithm">documentation</a> , polyline with precision 5), <code>polyline6</code> ( <a href="https://developers.google.com/maps/documentation/utilities/polylinealgorithm">documentation</a> , polyline with precision 6), <code>geojson</code> (as <a href="https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7946#appendix-A.2">LineString</a> ).</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>overview</code> <br> (optional)</td> 
            <td>Type of returned overview geometry. Allowed values are: <code>simplified</code> (default, a simplified version of the geometry), <code>full</code> (the most detailed geometry available), <code>false</code> (no overview geometry).</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>radiuses</code> <br> (optional)</td> 
            <td>Maximum distance in meters that each coordinate is allowed to move when snapped to a nearby road segment. There must be as many radiuses as there are coordinates in the request, each separated by <code>;</code> . Values can be any number greater than 0 or they can be the string <code>unlimited</code> . If no routable road is found within the radius, a <code>NoSegment</code> error is returned.</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>steps</code> <br> (optional)</td> 
            <td>Whether to return steps and turn-by-turn instructions. Allowed values are: <code>false</code> (default), <code>true</code></td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>bearings</code> <br> (optional)</td> 
            <td>Used to filter the road segment the waypoint will be placed on by direction and dictates the angle of approach. This option should always be used in conjunction with the <code>radiuses</code> parameter. The parameter takes two values per waypoint: the first is an angle clockwise from true north between 0 and 360. The second is the range of degrees the angle can deviate by. We recommend a value of 45° or 90° for the range, as bearing measurements tend to be inaccurate. This is useful for making sure we reroute vehicles on new routes that continue traveling in their current direction. A request that does this would provide bearing and radius values for the first waypoint and leave the remaining values empty. If provided, the list of bearings must be the same length as the list of waypoints, but you can skip a coordinate and show its position with the <code>;</code> separator.</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>annotations</code> <br> (optional)</td> 
            <td>Whether or not to return additional metadata along the route. Possible values are: <code>duration</code> , <code>distance</code> and <code>speed</code> . Several annotations can be used by separating them with <code>,</code> . See the <a href="#routeleg-object">RouteLeg object</a> for more details on what is included with annotations.</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>language</code> <br> (optional)</td> 
            <td>Language of returned turn-by-turn text instructions. See <a href="#instructions-languages">supported languages</a> . The default is <code>en</code> for English.</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>distributions</code> <br> (optional)</td> 
            <td>Specify pick-up and drop-off locations for a trip by providing a <code>;</code> delimited list of number pairs that correspond with the <code>coordinates</code> list. The first number indicates the index to the coordinate of the pick-up location in the coordinates list, and the second number indicates the index to the coordinate of the drop-off location in the coordinates list. Each pair must contain exactly two numbers. Pick-up and drop-off locations in one pair cannot be the same. The returned solution will visit pick-up locations before visiting drop-off locations. The depot (first location) can only be a pick-up location but not a drop-off location.</td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <p>Unrecognized options in the query string result in an <code>InvalidInput</code> error.</p> 
         <p>Note that routes returned by the Optimization API will behave as if <a href="#retrieve-directions">continue_straight=false</a> was set at each waypoint. See the <a href="#retrieve-directions">continue\straight</a> parameter for more details on what this means for the route.</p> 
         <p><strong>Fixing Start and End Points</strong></p> 
         <p>It is possible to explicitly set the start or end coordinate of the trip. When source<a href="https://mapbox.com/help/define-source/" title="A source supplies data to be shown on maps that use Mapbox GL. Sources are defined by the Mapbox Style Specification, and are used with style layers to visually represent the source data on to a map. Specific source types may not be supported depending on which platform you're developing on, so refer to platform-specific documentation when adding sources to your map." class="auto-glossary-link" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank">?</a> is set to <code>first</code>, the first coordinate is used as the start coordinate of the trip in the output. When destination is set to <code>last</code>, the last coordinate will be used as destination of the trip in the returned output. If you specify <code>any</code>, any of the coordinates can be used as the first or last coordinate in the output.</p> 
         <p>If <code>source=any&amp;destination=any</code> the returned roundtrip will still start at the first input coordinate by default.</p> 
         <p>Not all combinations of <code>roundtrip</code>, <code>source</code> and <code>destination</code> are supported. Right now, the following combinations are possible:</p> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th align="left">roundtrip</th> 
            <th align="left">source</th> 
            <th align="left">destination</th> 
            <th align="left">supported</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> 
           <tr> 
            <td align="left">true</td> 
            <td align="left">first</td> 
            <td align="left">last</td> 
            <td align="left"><strong>yes</strong></td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td align="left">true</td> 
            <td align="left">first</td> 
            <td align="left">any</td> 
            <td align="left"><strong>yes</strong></td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td align="left">true</td> 
            <td align="left">any</td> 
            <td align="left">last</td> 
            <td align="left"><strong>yes</strong></td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td align="left">true</td> 
            <td align="left">any</td> 
            <td align="left">any</td> 
            <td align="left"><strong>yes</strong></td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td align="left">false</td> 
            <td align="left">first</td> 
            <td align="left">last</td> 
            <td align="left"><strong>yes</strong></td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td align="left">false</td> 
            <td align="left">first</td> 
            <td align="left">any</td> 
            <td align="left">no</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td align="left">false</td> 
            <td align="left">any</td> 
            <td align="left">last</td> 
            <td align="left">no</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td align="left">false</td> 
            <td align="left">any</td> 
            <td align="left">any</td> 
            <td align="left">no</td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
        </div>
        <div class="space-bottom4 col6 pad2 prose clip fill-light space-top5" data-reactid="279">
         <div class="endpoint dark fill-dark round "> 
          <div class="round-left pad0y pad1x fill-lighten0 code small endpoint-method">
           GET
          </div> 
          <div class="pad0 code small endpoint-url">
           https://api.mapbox.com/optimized-trips/v1/
           <span class="strong">{profile}</span>/
           <span class="strong">{coordinates}</span>
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <h4 id="example-requests-1">Example requests</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs"><span class="hljs-comment"># request an optimized car trip with no additional options</span>
curl <span class="hljs-string">"https://api.mapbox.com/optimized-trips/v1/mapbox/driving/-122.42,37.78;-122.45,37.91;-122.48,37.73?access_token=<span class="token-widget"></span>"</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># request an optimized bicycle trip with steps and geojson response</span>
curl <span class="hljs-string">"https://api.mapbox.com/optimized-trips/v1/mapbox/cycling/-122.42,37.78;-122.45,37.91;-122.48,37.73?steps=true&amp;geometries=geojson&amp;access_token=<span class="token-widget"></span>"</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># request an optimized car roundtrip in Berlin with four coordinates, starting at the first coordinate pair, ending at the coordinate pair</span>
curl <span class="hljs-string">"https://api.mapbox.com/optimized-trips/v1/mapbox/driving/13.388860,52.517037;13.397634,52.529407;13.428555,52.523219;13.418555,52.523215?source=first&amp;destination=last&amp;roundtrip=true&amp;access_token=<span class="token-widget"></span>"</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># request an optimized car trip with four coordinates and one distributions constraint where the last given coordinate must be visited before the second</span>
curl <span class="hljs-string">"https://api.mapbox.com/optimized-trips/v1/mapbox/driving/13.388860,52.517037;13.397634,52.529407;13.428555,52.523219;13.418555,52.523215?roundtrip=true&amp;distributions=3,1&amp;access_token=<span class="token-widget"></span>"</span></pre> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Optimization response format" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="280">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="281">
         <h3 id="optimization-response-format">Optimization response format</h3> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>code</code>: String indicating the state of the response. This is a separate code than the HTTP status code. On normal valid responses, the value will be <code>Ok</code>. See the errors section below for more information.</li> 
          <li><code>waypoints</code>: Array of <code>waypoint</code> objects. Each waypoint is an input coordinate snapped to the road and path network. The waypoints appear in the array in the order of the input coordinates.</li> 
          <li><code>trips</code>: Array of <code>trip</code> objects. Will have zero or one trip.</li> 
         </ul> 
         <p><strong>Waypoint object</strong></p> 
         <p>An input coordinate snapped to the roads network.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li><code>name</code>: String with the name of the way the coordinate snapped to</li> 
          <li><code>location</code>: Array of <code>[ longitude, latitude ]</code> for the snapped coordinate</li> 
          <li><code>trips_index</code>: Index to the <code>trip</code> object in the <code>trips</code> array that contains this waypoint</li> 
          <li><code>waypoint_index</code>: Index of position of the waypoint within the <code>trip</code></li> 
         </ul> 
         <p><strong>Trip object</strong></p> 
         <p>A <code>trip</code> object is a route through (potentially multiple) waypoints. It follows the exact same format as the <code>Route object</code> in the Directions API. Please refer to the <a href="#directions">Directions API documentation</a>.</p> 
        </div>
        <div class="space-bottom4 col6 pad2 prose clip fill-light space-top5" data-reactid="282">
         <h4 id="example-response-26">Example response</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">{
    <span class="hljs-attr">"code"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"Ok"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"waypoints"</span>: [
        {
            <span class="hljs-attr">"location"</span>: [
                <span class="hljs-number">-6.80897</span>,
                <span class="hljs-number">62.000075</span>
            ],
            <span class="hljs-attr">"waypoint_index"</span>: <span class="hljs-number">0</span>,
            <span class="hljs-attr">"name"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"Kirkjubøarvegur"</span>,
            <span class="hljs-attr">"trips_index"</span>: <span class="hljs-number">0</span>
        },
        {
            <span class="hljs-attr">"location"</span>: [
                <span class="hljs-number">-6.802374</span>,
                <span class="hljs-number">62.004142</span>
            ],
            <span class="hljs-attr">"waypoint_index"</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>,
            <span class="hljs-attr">"name"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"Marknagilsvegur"</span>,
            <span class="hljs-attr">"trips_index"</span>: <span class="hljs-number">0</span>
        }
    ],
    <span class="hljs-attr">"trips"</span>: [
        {
            <span class="hljs-attr">"distance"</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1660.8</span>,

            <span class="hljs-attr">"legs"</span>: [
                {
                    <span class="hljs-attr">"summary"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">""</span>,

            ],
            <span class="hljs-attr">"geometry"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"oklyJ`{ph@yBuY_F{^_FxJoBrBs@d@mATlAUr@e@nBsB~EyJ~Ez^xBtY"</span>
        }
    ]
}</pre> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Optimization errors" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="283">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="284">
         <h3 id="optimization-errors">Optimization errors</h3> 
         <p>On error, the server responds with different HTTP status codes. For responses with HTTP status codes lower than <code>500</code>, the JSON response body includes the <code>code</code> property, which may be used by client programs to manage control flow. The response body may also include a <code>message</code> property, with a human-readable explanation of the error. If a server error occurs, the HTTP status code will be 500 or higher and the response will not include a <code>code</code> property.</p> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Response body <code>code</code></th> 
            <th>HTTP status code</th> 
            <th>comment</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>Ok</code></td> 
            <td><code>200</code></td> 
            <td>Normal success case</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>NoTrips</code></td> 
            <td><code>200</code></td> 
            <td>For one coordinate no route to other coordinates could be found. Check for impossible routes (e.g. routes over oceans without ferry connections).</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>NotImplemented</code></td> 
            <td><code>200</code></td> 
            <td>For the given combination of <code>source</code> , <code>destination</code> and <code>roundtrip</code> , this request is not supported.</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>ProfileNotFound</code></td> 
            <td><code>404</code></td> 
            <td>Use a valid profile as described <a href="#directions">above</a></td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>InvalidInput</code></td> 
            <td><code>422</code></td> 
            <td>The given request was not valid. The <code>message</code> key of the response will hold an explanation of the invalid input.</td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <p>All other properties might be undefined.</p> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Tokens" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="285">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="286">
         <h2 id="tokens">Tokens</h2> 
         <p>An <a href="#access-tokens">access token</a>, referred to hereafter as 'token', grants access to Mapbox resources on behalf of a user. All accounts have a public token by default. Additional tokens can be created to grant additional, or more limited, privileges.</p> 
         <p>To create additional tokens using this API you will first need to create an initial token. This initial token must contain the <code>tokens:write</code> scope and all scopes you want to add to the created token. To create the initial token visit your <a href="https://www.mapbox.com/studio/account/tokens/">Mapbox Studio API access tokens page</a>, and click <strong>Create a new token</strong>.</p> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="The token format" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="287">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="288">
         <h3 id="the-token-format">The token format</h3> 
         <p>Mapbox uses <a href="https://jwt.io/">JSON Web Tokens</a> (JWT) as the token format. Each token is a string delimited by dots into three parts: header, payload, and signature.</p> 
         <p>The <strong>header</strong> is a literal value of either <code>pk</code> (public token), <code>sk</code> (secret token), or <code>tk</code> (temporary token).</p> 
         <p>The <strong>payload</strong> is a base64-encoded JSON object containing the identity and authorities of the token. <code>pk</code> and <code>sk</code> tokens contain a reference to metadata which holds the rights granted for the token. <code>tk</code> tokens contain the content of the metadata directly in the payload.</p> 
         <p>The <strong>signature</strong> is signed by Mapbox and used to verify the token has not been tampered with.</p> 
         <p>The actions allowed by a token are based on <strong>scopes</strong>. A scope is a string that often is a resource type and action separated by a colon. For example, the <code>styles:read</code> scope allows read access to styles. Tokens will have access to different scopes depending on their account level and other features of their account.</p> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="The token metadata object" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="289">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="290">
         <h3 id="the-token-metadata-object">The token metadata object</h3> 
         <p>Every token has a metadata object that contains information about the capabilities of the token. Token metadata contains the following properties:</p> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Property</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>id</code></td> 
            <td>the identifier for the token</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>usage</code></td> 
            <td>the type of token</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>client</code></td> 
            <td>the client for the token, always 'api'</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>default</code></td> 
            <td>if the token is a default token</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>scopes</code></td> 
            <td>array of scopes granted to the token</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>note</code></td> 
            <td>human friendly description of the token</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>created</code></td> 
            <td>date and time the token was created</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>modified</code></td> 
            <td>date and time the token was last modified</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>token</code></td> 
            <td>the token itself</td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <p><strong>Limits</strong></p> 
         <ul> 
          <li>Requests must be made over HTTPS. HTTP is not supported.</li> 
          <li>The Tokens API is limited to 120 requests per minute per account.</li> 
         </ul> 
        </div>
        <div class="space-bottom4 col6 pad2 prose clip fill-light space-top5" data-reactid="291">
         <h4 id="the-token-metadata-object-1">The token metadata object</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">{
  <span class="hljs-attr">"id"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"cijucimbe000brbkt48d0dhcx"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"usage"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"pk"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"client"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"api"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"default"</span>: <span class="hljs-literal">false</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"note"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"My website"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"scopes"</span>: [<span class="hljs-string">"styles:read"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"fonts:read"</span>],
  <span class="hljs-attr">"created"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"2016-01-25T19:07:07.621Z"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"modified"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"2016-01-26T00:39:57.941Z"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"token"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"pk.eyJ1Ijoic2NvdGhpcyIsImEiOiJjaWp1Y2ltYmUwMDBicmJrdDQ4ZDBkaGN4In0.sbihZCZJ56-fsFNKHXF8YQ"</span>
}</pre> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="List tokens" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="292">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="293">

         <p>Lists all tokens for an account.</p> 
         <p>This endpoint supports <a href="#pagination">pagination</a>.</p> 
         <p>Note: The token property will not be included for <code>sk</code> tokens.</p> 
        </div>

          </div>

          </div> 
         </div>

       <div data-title="Create token" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="295">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="296">
         <h3 id="create-token">Create token</h3> 
         <p>Creates a new token.</p> 
         <p>Every requested scope must be present in the access token<a href="https://mapbox.com/help/define-access-token/" title="To use any of Mapbox's tools, APIs, or SDKs, you'll need a Mapbox access token. Mapbox uses access tokens to associate requests to API resources with your account. You can find all your access tokens, create new ones, or delete existing ones on your API access tokens page." class="auto-glossary-link" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank">?</a> used to allow the request. It is not possible to create a token with access to more scopes than the token that created it.</p> 
         <p>The scopes included in the token decide whether the token is public or secret. A public token may only contains public scopes.</p> 
        </div>
        <div class="space-bottom4 col6 pad2 prose clip fill-light space-top5" data-reactid="297">
         <div class="endpoint fill-dark round unround-topright dark"> 
          <div class="round-left pad0y pad1x fill-lighten0 code micro endpoint-method">
           POST
          </div> 
          <div class="pad0 code micro endpoint-url scroll-styled">
           /tokens/v2/
           <span class="strong">{username}</span>
          </div> 
          <div class="endpoint-token contain fill-lighten0 pad0x round-topright"> 
           <span class="pad0 micro code">tokens:write</span> 
           <a href="#access-tokens" class="fill-darken1 round-bottom pad0x center quiet line-height15 endpoint-scope space-top3 micro pin-top"> Token scope </a> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <h4 id="example-request-38">Example request</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">curl -X POST <span class="hljs-string">"https://api.mapbox.com/tokens/v2/{username}?access_token=<span class="token-widget"></span>"</span></pre> 
         <h4 id="example-request-body-6">Example request body</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">{
  <span class="hljs-attr">"scopes"</span>: [<span class="hljs-string">"styles:read"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"fonts:read"</span>],
  <span class="hljs-attr">"note"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"My top secret project"</span>
}</pre> 
         <h4 id="example-response-28">Example response</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">{
  <span class="hljs-attr">"client"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"api"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"note"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"My top secret project"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"usage"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"pk"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"id"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"cijucimbe000brbkt48d0dhcx"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"default"</span>: <span class="hljs-literal">false</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"scopes"</span>: [<span class="hljs-string">"styles:read"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"fonts:read"</span>],
  <span class="hljs-attr">"created"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"2016-01-25T19:07:07.621Z"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"modified"</span>:<span class="hljs-string">"2016-01-25T19:07:07.621Z"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"token"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"pk.eyJ1Ijoic2NvdGhpcyIsImEiOiJjaWp1Y2ltYmUwMDBicmJrdDQ4ZDBkaGN4In0.sbihZCZJ56-fsFNKHXF8YQ"</span>
}</pre> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Create temporary token" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="298">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="299">
         <h3 id="create-temporary-token">Create temporary token</h3> 
         <p>Creates a new temporary token that automatically expires at a fixed time.</p> 
         <p>The <code>expires</code> property for a temporary token cannot be in the past or more than 1 hour in the future. If the authorizing token is temporary, the <code>expires</code> cannot be later than that of the authorizing token.</p> 
         <p>Every requested scope must be present in the authorizing token used to allow the request. It is not possible to create a token with access to more scopes than the token that created it.</p> 
         <p>Unlike public and secret tokens, a temporary token contains its metadata inside the payload of the token instead of referencing a metadata object that persists on the server. Temporary tokens cannot be updated or revoked after they are created.</p> 
        </div>
        <div class="space-bottom4 col6 pad2 prose clip fill-light space-top5" data-reactid="300">
         <div class="endpoint fill-dark round unround-topright dark"> 
          <div class="round-left pad0y pad1x fill-lighten0 code micro endpoint-method">
           POST
          </div> 
          <div class="pad0 code micro endpoint-url scroll-styled">
           /tokens/v2/
           <span class="strong">{username}</span>
          </div> 
          <div class="endpoint-token contain fill-lighten0 pad0x round-topright"> 
           <span class="pad0 micro code">tokens:write</span> 
           <a href="#access-tokens" class="fill-darken1 round-bottom pad0x center quiet line-height15 endpoint-scope space-top3 micro pin-top"> Token scope </a> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <h4 id="example-request-39">Example request</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">curl -X POST <span class="hljs-string">"https://api.mapbox.com/tokens/v2/{username}?access_token=<span class="token-widget"></span>"</span></pre> 
         <h4 id="example-request-body-7">Example request body</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">{
  <span class="hljs-attr">"expires"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"2016-09-15T19:27:53.000Z"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"scopes"</span>: [<span class="hljs-string">"styles:read"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"fonts:read"</span>]
}</pre> 
         <h4 id="example-response-29">Example response</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">{
  <span class="hljs-attr">"token"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"tk.eyJ1IjoibWFwYm94IiwiZXhwIjoxNDczOTY3NjczLCJpYXQiOjE0NzM5Njc2NDMsInNjb3BlcyI6WyJzdHlsZXM6cmVhZCIsImZvbnRzOnJlYWQiXSwiY2xpZW50IjoiYXBpIn0.ZepsWvpjTMlpePE4IQBs0g"</span>
}</pre> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Update a token" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="301">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="302">
         <h3 id="update-a-token">Update a token</h3> 
         <p>Update note or scopes in a token's metadata.</p> 
         <p>A public, <code>pk</code>, token may only be updated to include other public scopes. A secret, <code>sk</code>, token may be updated to contain public and secret scopes.</p> 
         <p>When updating scopes for an existing token, the token sent along with the request must also have the scopes you're requesting. It is not possible to create a token with access to more scopes than the token that updated it.</p> 
        </div>
        <div class="space-bottom4 col6 pad2 prose clip fill-light space-top5" data-reactid="303">
         <div class="endpoint fill-dark round unround-topright dark"> 
          <div class="round-left pad0y pad1x fill-lighten0 code micro endpoint-method">
           PATCH
          </div> 
          <div class="pad0 code micro endpoint-url scroll-styled">
           /tokens/v2/
           <span class="strong">{username}</span>/
           <span class="strong">{token_id}</span>
          </div> 
          <div class="endpoint-token contain fill-lighten0 pad0x round-topright"> 
           <span class="pad0 micro code">tokens:write</span> 
           <a href="#access-tokens" class="fill-darken1 round-bottom pad0x center quiet line-height15 endpoint-scope space-top3 micro pin-top"> Token scope </a> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <h4 id="example-request-40">Example request</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">curl -X PATCH  <span class="hljs-string">"https://api.mapbox.com/tokens/v2/{username}/{token_id}?access_token=<span class="token-widget"></span>"</span></pre> 
         <h4 id="example-request-body-8">Example request body</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">{
  <span class="hljs-attr">"scopes"</span>: [<span class="hljs-string">"styles:tiles"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"styles:read"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"fonts:read"</span>]
}</pre> 
         <h4 id="example-response-30">Example response</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">{
  <span class="hljs-attr">"client"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"api"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"note"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"My top secret project"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"usage"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"pk"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"id"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"cijucimbe000brbkt48d0dhcx"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"default"</span>: <span class="hljs-literal">false</span>,

}</pre> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Delete a token" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="304">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="305">
         <h3 id="delete-a-token">Delete a token</h3> 
         <p>Revoke a token's authorization, removing its access to Mapbox APIs. This is the same as deleting a token. Applications using the revoked token will need to get a new access token<a href="https://mapbox.com/help/define-access-token/" title="To use any of Mapbox's tools, APIs, or SDKs, you'll need a Mapbox access token. Mapbox uses access tokens to associate requests to API resources with your account. You can find all your access tokens, create new ones, or delete existing ones on your API access tokens page." class="auto-glossary-link" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank">?</a> before they can access Mapbox APIs.</p> 
         <p>Note: Cached resources may continue to be accessible for a short period after a token is revoked. No new or updated resources will be accessible with the revoked token.</p> 
        </div>
        <div class="space-bottom4 col6 pad2 prose clip fill-light space-top5" data-reactid="306">
         <div class="endpoint fill-dark round unround-topright dark"> 
          <div class="round-left pad0y pad1x fill-lighten0 code micro endpoint-method">
           DELETE
          </div> 
          <div class="pad0 code micro endpoint-url scroll-styled">
           /tokens/v2/
           <span class="strong">{username}</span>/
           <span class="strong">{token_id}</span>
          </div> 
          <div class="endpoint-token contain fill-lighten0 pad0x round-topright"> 
           <span class="pad0 micro code">tokens:write</span> 
           <a href="#access-tokens" class="fill-darken1 round-bottom pad0x center quiet line-height15 endpoint-scope space-top3 micro pin-top"> Token scope </a> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <h4 id="example-request-41">Example request</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">curl -X DELETE <span class="hljs-string">"https://api.mapbox.com/tokens/v2/{username}/{token_id}?access_token=<span class="token-widget"></span>"</span></pre> 
         <h4 id="example-response-31">Example response</h4> 
         <blockquote> 
          <p>HTTP 204</p> 
         </blockquote> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Retrieve a token" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="307">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="308">
         <h3 id="retrieve-a-token">Retrieve a token</h3> 
         <p>Check if a token is valid. If the token is invalid an explanation of why is returned as the <code>code</code> property.</p> 
         <p>The body of the token is parsed and included as the <code>token</code> property in object form.</p> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Code</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>TokenValid</code></td> 
            <td>the token is valid and active</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>TokenMalformed</code></td> 
            <td>the token can not be parsed</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>TokenInvalid</code></td> 
            <td>the signature for the token does not validate</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>TokenExpired</code></td> 
            <td>the token was temporary and expired</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>TokenRevoked</code></td> 
            <td>the token's authorization has been revoked</td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
        </div>
        <div class="space-bottom4 col6 pad2 prose clip fill-light space-top5" data-reactid="309">
         <div class="endpoint dark fill-dark round "> 
          <div class="round-left pad0y pad1x fill-lighten0 code small endpoint-method">
           GET
          </div> 
          <div class="pad0 code small endpoint-url">
           /tokens/v2?access_token=
           <span class="strong"><span class="token-widget"></span></span>
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <h4 id="example-request-42">Example request</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">$ curl <span class="hljs-string">"https://api.mapbox.com/tokens/v2?access_token=<span class="token-widget"></span>"</span></pre> 
         <h4 id="example-response-for-a-public-token">Example response for a public token</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">{
  <span class="hljs-attr">"code"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"TokenValid"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"token"</span>: {
    <span class="hljs-attr">"usage"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"pk"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"user"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"mapbox"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"authorization"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"cijucimbe000brbkt48d0dhcx"</span>
  }
}</pre> 
         <h4 id="example-response-for-a-temporary-token">Example response for a temporary token</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">{
  <span class="hljs-attr">"code"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"TokenExpired"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"token"</span>: {
    <span class="hljs-attr">"usage"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"tk"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"user"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"mapbox"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"expires"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"2016-09-15T19:27:53.000Z"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"created"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"2016-09-15T19:27:23.000Z"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"scopes"</span>: [<span class="hljs-string">"styles:read"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"fonts:read"</span>],
    <span class="hljs-attr">"client"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"api"</span>
  }
}</pre> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="List scopes" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix " data-reactid="310">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="311">
         <h3 id="list-scopes">List scopes</h3> 
         <p>List scopes for a user. All potential scopes a user has access to are listed.</p> 
         <p>Public tokens may only contain scopes with the <code>public</code> property set to <code>true</code>. Secret tokens may contain any scope.</p> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Property</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>id</code></td> 
            <td>identifier of the scope</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>description</code></td> 
            <td>human friendly description of the scope</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>public</code></td> 
            <td><code>true</code> if the scope is available for public tokens</td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
        </div>
        <div class="space-bottom4 col6 pad2 prose clip fill-light space-top5" data-reactid="312">
         <div class="endpoint fill-dark round unround-topright dark"> 
          <div class="round-left pad0y pad1x fill-lighten0 code micro endpoint-method">
           GET
          </div> 
          <div class="pad0 code micro endpoint-url scroll-styled">
           /scopes/v1/
           <span class="strong">{username}</span>?access_token=
           <span class="strong"><span class="token-widget"></span></span>
          </div> 
          <div class="endpoint-token contain fill-lighten0 pad0x round-topright"> 
           <span class="pad0 micro code">scopes:list</span> 
           <a href="#access-tokens" class="fill-darken1 round-bottom pad0x center quiet line-height15 endpoint-scope space-top3 micro pin-top"> Token scope </a> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <h4 id="example-request-43">Example request</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">$ curl <span class="hljs-string">"https://api.mapbox.com/scopes/v1/{username}?access_token=<span class="token-widget"></span>"</span></pre> 
         <h4 id="example-response-truncated">Example response (truncated)</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">[
  {
    <span class="hljs-attr">"id"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"scopes:list"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"description"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"List all available scopes."</span>
  },
  {
    <span class="hljs-attr">"id"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"styles:read"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"public"</span>: <span class="hljs-literal">true</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">"description"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"Read styles."</span>
  }
]</pre> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Analytics" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix preview" data-reactid="313">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="314">
         <h2 id="analytics">Analytics</h2> 
         <p><em>This API is available for <a href="https://www.mapbox.com/pricing/">Commercial and Enterprise</a> plans.</em></p> 
         <p>The Mapbox Analytics API returns API usage for services by resource. For example, it can calculate the number of geocoding<a href="https://mapbox.com/help/define-geocoding/" title="Geocoding is the process of taking an address or name of a place and converting it into latitude and longitude values. The Mapbox Geocoding API allows you to performs two types of geocoding: forward geocoding and reverse geocoding." class="auto-glossary-link" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank">?</a> requests made in a week with a specific access token<a href="https://mapbox.com/help/define-access-token/" title="To use any of Mapbox's tools, APIs, or SDKs, you'll need a Mapbox access token. Mapbox uses access tokens to associate requests to API resources with your account. You can find all your access tokens, create new ones, or delete existing ones on your API access tokens page." class="auto-glossary-link" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank">?</a>.</p> 
        </div>
       </div>
       <div data-title="Retrieve analytics" class="keyline-top section contain clearfix preview" data-reactid="315">
        <div class="space-bottom8 col6 pad2x prose clip" data-reactid="316">
         <h3 id="retrieve-analytics">Retrieve analytics</h3> 
         <p>Returns the request counts per day for given resource and period.</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li>If the <code>{resourceType}</code> is <code>tokens</code>, the <code>{id}</code> is the complete token.</li> 
          <li>If the <code>{resourceType}</code> is <code>styles</code>, the <code>{id}</code> is the Style ID. Not to be confused with the Style <em>URL</em>, the id is the alphanumeric segment at the end of the style: the Style URL <code>mapbox://styles/user/cimdoca6f00</code> contains the Style ID <code>cimdoca6f00</code>, so the analytics request would have the path <code>/analytics/v1/styles/user/cimdoca6f00</code>.</li> 
          <li>If the <code>{resourceType}</code> is <code>tilesets</code>, the <code>{id}</code> is a Map ID.</li> 
         </ul> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>URL Parameter</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>resourceType</code></td> 
            <td>The resource being requested. Valid resource types are <code>accounts</code> , <code>tokens</code> , <code>tilesets</code> or <code>styles</code> .</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>username</code></td> 
            <td>The username for the account that owns the resource.</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>id</code> <br> (optional)</td> 
            <td>The id for the resource. In the case of <code>accounts</code> this isn't required.</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>period</code> <br> (optional)</td> 
            <td>2 comma separated dates as <a href="#dates">ISO formatted strings</a> . The first date must be earlier than the second. The period is inclusive of dates provided. Defaults to last 90 days if not provided. The maximum period is 1 year. If the provided dates are more than 1 year apart, an error will be returned.</td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <p>Responses include arrays of request counts per service.</p> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Property</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>timestamps</code></td> 
            <td>an array of dates as ISO formatted strings for each day included in the response.</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>period</code></td> 
            <td>a 2 element array with start and end dates as ISO formatted strings for the response period.</td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>services</code></td> 
            <td>an object with a key per service the value of which is an array of request counts per day in the same sequence as <code>timestamps</code> .</td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <p>Only services applicable to the given resource are returned in the response.</p> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Resource type</th> 
            <th>Services returned in response</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accounts</code></td> 
            <td><code>mapview</code> <code>static</code> <code>tile</code> <code>directions</code> <code>geocode</code></td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>tokens</code></td> 
            <td><code>mapview</code> <code>static</code> <code>tile</code> <code>directions</code> <code>geocode</code></td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>tilesets</code></td> 
            <td><code>mapview</code> <code>static</code> <code>tile</code></td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>styles</code></td> 
            <td><code>mapview</code> <code>static</code> <code>tile</code></td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <p>For the <code>styles</code> resource type, Static &amp; Tile services refer to the <a href="#static">Static API</a>. For <code>tilesets</code>, Static &amp; Tile services refer to the <a href="#static-classic">Static (Classic)</a> and <a href="#retrieve-tiles">Maps ? Tiles</a> APIs.</p> 
        </div>
        <div class="space-bottom4 col6 pad2 prose clip fill-light space-top5" data-reactid="317">
         <div class="endpoint fill-dark round unround-topright dark"> 
          <div class="round-left pad0y pad1x fill-lighten0 code micro endpoint-method">
           GET
          </div> 
          <div class="pad0 code micro endpoint-url scroll-styled">
           /analytics/v1/
           <span class="strong">{resourceType}</span>/
           <span class="strong">{username}</span>/
           <span class="strong">{id}</span>?period=
           <span class="strong">{period}</span>
          </div> 
          <div class="endpoint-token contain fill-lighten0 pad0x round-topright"> 
           <span class="pad0 micro code">analytics:read</span> 
           <a href="#access-tokens" class="fill-darken1 round-bottom pad0x center quiet line-height15 endpoint-scope space-top3 micro pin-top"> Token scope </a> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <h4 id="example-request-44">Example Request</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">curl <span class="hljs-string">"https://api.mapbox.com/analytics/v1/tilesets/mapbox/mapbox.streets?period=2016-03-22T00:00:00.000Z,2016-03-24T00:00:00.000Z&amp;access_token=<span class="token-widget"></span>"</span></pre> 
         <h4 id="example-response-32">Example response</h4> 
         <pre class="hljs">{
    <span class="hljs-attr">"period"</span>: [<span class="hljs-string">"2016-03-22T00:00:00.000Z"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"2016-03-24T00:00:00.000Z"</span>],
    <span class="hljs-attr">"timestamps"</span>: [<span class="hljs-string">"2016-03-22T00:00:00.000Z"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"2016-03-23T00:00:00.000Z"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"2016-03-24T00:00:00.000Z"</span>],
    <span class="hljs-attr">"services"</span>: {
        <span class="hljs-attr">"mapview"</span>: [ <span class="hljs-number">25</span>, <span class="hljs-number">22</span>, <span class="hljs-number">37</span> ],
        <span class="hljs-attr">"static"</span>: [ <span class="hljs-number">23</span>, <span class="hljs-number">20</span>, <span class="hljs-number">34</span> ],
        <span class="hljs-attr">"tiles"</span>: [ <span class="hljs-number">30</span>, <span class="hljs-number">39</span>, <span class="hljs-number">53</span> ]
    }
}</pre> 
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
